This option prevents the profile from getting stuck at a given step.\n\n### IMPROVED\n\n* In sequential audiences, you can’t add another step if the final step uses ‘did not perform the event’. This prevents creating invalid sequences.\n\n### FIXED\n\n* We’ve fixed an issue where you could save an audience with an empty value in dropdown (enum) attributes. Now, dropdown attributes require a selection, while free-text attributes can still be left blank.\n* We fixed Google Ads Customer Match activations that could send profiles without any of the selected identifiers. Now, those profiles aren’t sent to Google Ads, which helps prevent Google-side errors and failed batches.\n\n## Data Collection\n\n### FIXED\n\n* We fixed session timeout handling on shared devices. This lets you work with consent data while using third-party consent management tools.\n* Device definitions for the device type, brand, and model dimensions in Analytics now refresh every two weeks. This improves device reporting accuracy.\n\n### FIXED\n\n* We fixed two chart issues when comparing February to the previous month: dates were shown as February 6, and tooltips didn’t appear on hover. You can now see correct daily breakdowns and hover tooltips for February comparison charts.\n* We fixed an issue that prevented sorting in the report preview when columns were duplicated. You can now sort columns in preview mode without errors.\n* We fixed infinite loading when reselecting the same dimension value in the report preview. You can now preview reports without loading delays across all chart types.\n* We fixed the missing \"No data available\" text in dashboard PDF exports when using list layout.\n* We fixed an issue where clicking a line chart note marker didn’t open the notes sidebar. You can now click note markers on charts to open the sidebar with the related note highlighted.\n* We fixed two issues in the scheduled reports list: search input lag with large datasets and unintended filtering when changing page size. You can now get faster search results and reliable filtering when managing scheduled reports.\n* We fixed the alert condition value multiplied or divided by 100 when switching between percentage and absolute conditions. You can now switch between them without unexpected value changes.\n* We fixed an issue where the share button became disabled after navigating from the SharePoint tab todashboards or real-time dashboards. The share button now stays enabled regardless of how you navigate.\n* We fixed an issue where alert email metric names appeared as untranslated keys instead of readable labels. Alert emails now show proper metric names in the UI.\n* We added input validation to the session log, quick search, and tracker debugger. You’ll now see clear error messages if copied-and-pasted input has formatting issues.\n\n## Data Activation\n\n### NEW\n\n* We’ve introduced a new audience type: sequential audiences. It lets you collect and activate audiences based on a defined sequence of completed actions, ideal for step-by-step workflows like form submissions and completed transactions.\n\n### IMPROVED\n\n* We now calculate audience membership based on when a user first joins an audience and is no longer extended by later qualifying activity. For example, with a 30-day duration, a user remains in the audience for up to 30 days from join time.","html":"\u003cstyle>/*! tailwindcss v4.1.17 | MIT License | https://tailwindcss.com */\n@layer theme, base, components, utilities;\n@layer utilities;\n\u003c/style>\u003ch2 class=\"heading heading-2 header-scroll\">\u003cdiv class=\"heading-anchor anchor waypoint\" id=\"analytics\">\u003c/div>\u003cdiv class=\"heading-text\">Analytics\u003c/div>\u003ca aria-label=\"Skip link to Analytics\" class=\"heading-anchor-icon fa fa-regular fa-anchor\" href=\"#analytics\">\u003c/a>\u003c/h2>\n\u003ch3 class=\"heading heading-3 header-scroll\">\u003cdiv class=\"heading-anchor anchor waypoint\" id=\"improved\">\u003c/div>\u003cdiv class=\"heading-text\">IMPROVED\u003c/div>\u003ca aria-label=\"Skip link to IMPROVED\" class=\"heading-anchor-icon fa fa-regular fa-anchor\" href=\"#improved\">\u003c/a>\u003c/h3>\n\u003cul>\n\u003cli>Analytics now shows consent-related reports, dimensions, and metrics even without Consent Manager in the license. You can now preview reports without loading delays across all chart types.\u003c/li>\n\u003cli>We fixed the missing &quot;No data available&quot; text in dashboard PDF exports when using list layout.\u003c/li>\n\u003cli>We fixed an issue where clicking a line chart note marker didn’t open the notes sidebar. You can now click note markers on charts to open the sidebar with the related note highlighted.\u003c/li>\n\u003cli>We fixed two issues in the scheduled reports list: search input lag with large datasets and unintended filtering when changing page size. You can now get faster search results and reliable filtering when managing scheduled reports.\u003c/li>\n\u003cli>We fixed the alert condition value multiplied or divided by 100 when switching between percentage and absolute conditions. You can now switch between them without unexpected value changes.\u003c/li>\n\u003cli>We fixed an issue where the share button became disabled after navigating from the SharePoint tab todashboards or real-time dashboards. The share button now stays enabled regardless of how you navigate.\u003c/li>\n\u003cli>We fixed an issue where alert email metric names appeared as untranslated keys instead of readable labels. Alert emails now show proper metric names in the UI.\u003c/li>\n\u003cli>We added input validation to the session log, quick search, and tracker debugger.
